## Completed Setup

- Clean p25 workspace cloned from `JaneShi99/pomerance-p24`.
- Built `src/pomerance` with Apple clang `-O3`.
- Verified known p23 and p24 triples with latest official DANGER3 `vpp.py` from remote `HEAD` `a65658b7b194546957fa62f40d60ca63efc37f93`: both `True`.
- Smoke-tested p25 `x16halvenonsplit`: code path works, reports `k=42` and the expected three odd parts.
- Added reusable detached launcher `src/launch_fleet_detached.py`.
- Added live status helpers `src/run_status_heartbeat.sh` and `src/launch_status_heartbeat.py`; `tail -f "$run_dir/watch.log"` now shows heartbeat status lines.
- Added tmux foreground watcher wrapper `src/launch_fleet_foreground_watch.sh`, but tmux cannot access `Documents` in this macOS permission context; use the Python launcher.
- Added `research/p25/p25_transfer_matrix.md`.
- Added `research/p25/p25_moonshot_lit_search_screening_matrix.md` and
  `research/p25/p25_moonshot_lit_search_first_hits_20260613.md`; three

The sparse local solution `A=(1+D+D^2)X^3Y` has support `3` but degree `3`; forcing degree zero fixes `c=-3/507` and makes the solution dense on all `507` quotient classes. For the correction `-A`, the degree-zero representative is exactly the scalar-balance escape `-A + (3/507)1`, with full raw block support `12675/12675`.
- Added `research/p25/p25_laneB_square_axis_raw_antiderivative_trace_gate.py` and `subsqrt_moonshot_laneB_square_axis_raw_antiderivative_trace.md`; the raw `C_25` sparse-section antiderivative makes the raw `D` boundary only two points, but it still has raw degree `75 = 25*3`. Trace-zero kernel modes do not change this degree. Forcing raw degree zero adds the same nonzero scalar to every raw source point, making both the block lift and sparse-section lift dense on all `12675` raw positions and their quotient traces dense on all `507` classes. Thus a raw escape must do more than choose a sparse kernel representative.
- Added `research/p25/p25_laneB_square_axis_selected_kernel_balance_gate.py` and `subsqrt_moonshot_laneB_square_axis_selected_kernel_balance.md`; the full selected-defect kernel is row-constant, not only global scalar. It can reduce degree-zero balance from full scalar support `507` to a minimum of one dense row plus two anomaly points, support `171` and raw block support `4275`, but it never changes the visible selected-defect anomaly and fails the raw producer contract for every row-constant choice. A fixed inversion witness gives sums `2*r_0` and `2*r_0-1` on two right-zero off-axis inversion pairs.

The completed six-point row has q-support `{25,138,197,310,369,482}`, degree zero, row sums zero, inversion sums `{0}`, and is anti-invariant under inversion in both the quotient and raw split fields.

It maps the top fiber `b=9`, trace-zero partner slice to the bottom fiber `b=3`, trace-one anomaly slice; its weighted Fourier zeros are exactly `{0,169,338}`, so there is no hidden low-frequency or proper-quotient compression.

  arithmetic producer.

   Latest bridge refinement: the recorded Hilbert-90 corner branch is now a row-labeled two-sign triangle law. Among the thirteen lifts of the same `C_13` shadow, the two corner graph witnesses have shapes `(3,141,25)` and `(25,141,3)`, both projectively `(1,18,150)`, and the other twelve lifts have no row-balanced half-bridge corner witnesses. The remaining producer debt is no longer lift selection; it is the raw `K` trace/block lift and Kummer cost.
56. Bridge Hilbert-90 source-chain corner raw `K` trace is now explicit: the active half-bridge corner requires the 25-point raw `K`-trace block lift. The block lift is trace-correct, kernel-trivial, and raw `D^3=Y` compatible on all four active corner chains. Sparse sections are trace-correct but expose all `25` kernel modes and break raw `D^3=Y`; hidden kernel modes do not repair the relation or trace contract. 117. McCarthy transformed quotient is now explicit: because the transformed main sum is nonzero on all `507` twists, the ratio `R(q)=LHS(q)/main_sum(q)` is defined and `R(q)-1` is supported exactly at `q=138`, with outer `S` image `(138,310,482)`. This is a sparse multiplicative reading of the theorem cancellation. However `R(138)=1790844` has order `79131=39*2029`, is not in `mu_507` or `mu_2028`, and `R(138)-1` has full auxiliary-field order `20574060`; the direct character-valued unit phase is killed unless a further identity cancels or explains the additive-root `2029` component before raw lift.
118. McCarthy power descent is now explicit: raising the sparse quotient to the additive-root order preserves singleton support and kills the additive component. Concretely `R(q)^2029 - 1` is supported exactly at `q=138`, `R(138)^2029=zeta_39^5` has order `39`, and the outer `S` image is still `(138,310,482)`. The wrong branch `R^39` keeps order `2029`, and `R^(39*2029)-1` is zero everywhere. This is the best current McCarthy/Barnes target: justify the `2029`th powered quotient, avoid arbitrary normalization of `zeta_39^5-1`, then connect the order-39 singleton to the p25 raw-Y closure.
119. McCarthy power coefficient transport to raw-Y is now explicit: the order-39 value descends canonically to `F_2029` via the local primitive-root convention, with `zeta_39=2^52=1358`, `zeta_39^5=1376`, `zeta_39^5-1=1375`, and inverse `636`. The unnormalized powered quotient keeps the right support but gives anomaly payload `656` and fails the raw-Y harness; multiplying by the determined inverse gives anomaly projector coefficient `1`, the all-one corrected seed payload, exact canonical quotient packet, raw support `6300`, and a passing ray-local raw-Y harness. The remaining debt is arithmetic justification of `R^2029` and this coefficient normalization inside the producer, not finite payload geometry.
120. McCarthy power cost ledger is now explicit: the remaining operation is not killed by p25 sub-sqrt accounting. Binary exponentiation for `2029` costs `18` multiplications; conservative copy bounds are `2029*3=6087` for the `S` trace, `2029*252=511308` for the quotient packet, `2029*507=1028703` for dense twist space, `2029*6300=12782700` for raw-Y support, and even `2029*12675=25717575` for the full raw order. The worst bound is below `sqrt(p)=3162277660168` by factor `122961`. The remaining debt is arithmetic legitimacy of the powered normalized quotient, not payload size.
121. McCarthy q-power projection law is now explicit: `x -> x^2029` on the auxiliary value field is a multiplicative projection, not a field Frobenius. It fixes `mu_2028` and `mu_39`, kills `mu_2029`, and sends the unused `mu_5` factor to fourth power. The target quotient decomposes as `R(138)=zeta_39^5 * additive_root^1475`, so `R(138)^2029=zeta_39^5`; a nonadditivity witness shows `(2+3)^2029 != 2^2029+3^2029` in `F_20574061`. The right theorem target is therefore: produce a multiplicative unit quotient first, then apply q-power projection and the determined coefficient normalization.
122. McCarthy additive-character gauge stability is now explicit: for representative gauges `u=1,2,13,-1`, the Gauss-transform law `g_u(A)=bar(A)(u)g_1(A)` holds across all `2028` character exponents, the h=2 row probes stay `R(129)=1`, `R(138)=1790844`, `R(147)=1`, and the projected value stays `R(138)^2029=12801419=zeta_39^5` of order `39`. The powered target is therefore not an artifact of the auxiliary additive-character choice; the remaining debt is still arithmetic unit-quotient legitimacy.
123. McCarthy idempotent-unit structure is now explicit: after q-power projection and coefficient transport, the target is the pointwise unit `U(q)=1+(zeta_39^5-1)*e_138(q)` in functions on `C_507` over `F_2029`, with `zeta_39^5=1376`, `zeta_39^5-1=1375`, inverse `636`, point support `1`, `U-1` support `1`, and pointwise order `39`. 125. 126. 170. Kubert-Lang reflection bridge is now explicit: the legal anti-invariant pairs do feed the KSY `T`-edge packet because the positive segment is symmetric.  With `C=base+D=(2,28)`, the relation `T=-2C` holds, `T/2=-C=(1,141)`, and the segment is `C-D,C,C+D`.  The KSY denominator set `C+jD+T=-C+jD` is the same as the inversion-pair denominator set `-(C+jD)=-C-jD`, with the two outer denominators swapped.  Thus `prod_j [C+jD]/[C+jD+T]` and `prod_j [C+jD]/[-C-jD]` are the same signed divisor.  A theorem source may target anti-invariant Siegel/Robert pair quotients, but it must also prove this reflection bridge and keep the forced `K` trace plus period-156 theta2 certificate.

by either proper axis alone.  Its pushforwards to modulus `3` and modulus `13`
both vanish, while pullback tests from `3` and `13` fail at residues
`1/7` and `1/14` respectively.  Indexed as `mod 3` rows against the nonzero
`mod 13` columns, the two rows are negatives, all row and column sums vanish,
and the row differences are not constant, so the word is not an additive
separation `A(mod 3)+B(mod 13)`.  The exact surviving structure is the tensor
`U_chi(r)=-chi_3(r)*chi_13(r)`.  This sharpens source-theorem filtering:
accept mixed `chi_3 tensor chi_13` character units, reject conductor-`3` only,
conductor-`13` only, projection-only, pullback-only, or additive-separated
explanations.  It is still not a finite-field value/divisor theorem or DANGER3
extraction.  The gate reports
`U_chi_is_genuine_mixed_chi3_tensor_chi13_character=1`,
`proper_axis_pushforwards_vanish_and_pullbacks_fail=1`, and
`ksy_y_yang_y507_conductor39_mixed_tensor_character_rows=1/1`.

259. Yang `Y_507` conductor-`39` coset selector is now executable: the

`12`, and the positive layer is the coset `7<2>`.  Thus
`U_chi=1_{7<2>}-1_{<2>}`, with
`<2>=(1,2,4,5,8,10,11,16,20,22,25,32)` and

and `p^2` preserves them; this explains `Frob_p(U_chi)=-U_chi` in the compact

260. Yang `Y_507` conductor-`39` coset Frobenius pairing is now executable:
the compact quotient has an exact cyclic descent contract.  Write
`H=<2>` in `(Z/39Z)^*` and
`Q=prod_{h in H} E_{7h}/E_h`, so `U_chi=1_{7H}-1_H`.  For p25,
`p mod 39 = 23 = 7*2^11`, `p*7 = 5 = 2^9`, and
`p^2 = 22 = 2^8`.  Therefore, for `h_i=2^i`,
`Frob_p(h_i)=7h_{i+11}`, `Frob_p(7h_i)=h_{i+9}`, and `Frob_p^2`
rotates both layers by `+8`.  In value language, this gives the clean
contract `Frob_p(Q)=Q^-1`; the period-norm word is
`W=6*U_chi=(1-Frob_p)(3*U_chi)`, equivalently `Q^6=(1-Frob_p)(Q^3)`.
This is a descent target, not yet a finite-field value/divisor theorem or

274. `X_1(8112)` torsion-gluing contract is now executable: the bridge target

317. Ray-local / conductor-39 alignment check is now executable.  It compares
the ray-local `theta31` finite payload with the conductor-`39` source object

the tempting shortcut is false: `U_chi` is not the raw theta31 payload or the

`U_chi` column sums, and raw signed dot product `0`.  After removing the pure
C-axis component from theta31, the mixed comparison still has dot product `0`,
with `theta31_mixed_rank=2`, `u_chi_rank=1`, combined rank `3`,
non-proportional ratios `{-2,-1,0,1,2}`, and six nonzero theta mixed cells
where `U_chi` vanishes.  Practical verdict: conductor-39 theorems are

`U_chi` implies theta31 needs an explicit bridge or value theorem.  The gate
reports `ksy_y_ray_local_conductor39_alignment_rows=1/1`.

scanned; none match raw or mixed theta31 support, with maximum intersection
only `12` cells and histograms `((10,288), (11,288), (12,360))` for raw
theta31 and `((10,432), (12,504))` for the mixed projection.  The exact
linear ansatz `target=a*U_chi+row+column` is inconsistent over `Q` for raw
theta31 and for mixed theta31, both with `39` equations, `16` variables, rank
`16`, and `8` inconsistent rows.  Separated multiplicative gauges preserve
mixed rank at most `1`, while theta31 has mixed rank `2`.  Practical verdict:
bare renaming, affine relabeling, row/column normalization, and separated
character gauges cannot turn `U_chi` into theta31.  The live conductor-`39`
